                print("You can only enter numbers for age")

import java.util.Scanner;

public class DigitExtractor {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner dig = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.print("Enter an integer: ");
        int number = dig.nextInt();
        System.out.println("Individual digits:");
        List list = new List();
        while (number > 0) {
            int digit = number % 10;
            System.out.println(digit);
            number /= 10;
            list.add(digit);
            System.out.println(digit);

        }
        System.out.println(list);
    }
}

		String cmdNum = args[0];
		for(int j=0 ; j< cmdNum.length(); j++){
			System.out.print(cmdNum.charAt(j)+" 	");
		}
		System.out.println();
		Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
		System.out.print("Enter a Number : ");
		String inputNum = input.nextLine();
		for (byte i=0; i < inputNum.length() ; i++){

		}
	}
}

[2023-03-14, 20:21:30] Deelaka Dias: public class Queue {
    public static void main(String[] args) {

    }
    private int front;
    private int rear;
    private int noOfItems;
    private int maxSize;
    private float[] queueArray;

    public void Queue(int size){
        maxSize = size;
        front = 0;
        rear = -1;
        noOfItems = 0;
        queueArray = new float[maxSize];
    }

    //isFull and isEmpty methods
    public boolean isFull () {
        return (rear + 1 == maxSize);
    }

    public boolean isEmpty () {
        return (noOfItems == 0);
    }

    //Enqueue
    public void enqueue (Float item){
        if (isFull()) {
            System.out.println("You have enter maximum number of shares to the program");
        } else {
            queueArray[++rear] = item;
            noOfItems++;
        }
    }

    //Dequeue
    public float dequeue () {
        if (isEmpty()) {
            System.out.println("You have successfully sold all stocks");
            return -1;
        } else {
            noOfItems--;
            return queueArray[front++];
        }

    }

    public float peek(){
        return queueArray[front];
    }
}

[2023-03-21, 19:37:51] Haleef IIT: import java.util.Scanner;
class Queue {
    int front;
    public int rear;
    public int noOfItems;
    private int maxSize;
    public float[] queueArray;
    public int count = 0;

    public void Queue(int size) {
        maxSize = size;
        front = 0;
        rear = -1;
        noOfItems = 0;
        queueArray = new float[maxSize];
    }

    //isFull and isEmpty methods
    public boolean isFull() {
        return (rear + 1 == maxSize);
    }

    public boolean isEmpty() {
        return (noOfItems == 0);
    }

    //Enqueue method
    public void enqueue(float item) {
        if (isFull()) {
            System.out.println("You have entered the total number of transactions you ");   //complete the output for isfull
        } else {
            queueArray[++rear] = item;
            noOfItems++;
        }
    }

    //Dequeue method
    public float dequeue() {
        if (isEmpty()) {
            //int remaining = (int) noOfSellingShares;
            //System.out.println("You need this" + " " + remaining + " " + "amount of more shares");
            System.out.println();
            return 0;
        } else {
            noOfItems--;
            return queueArray[front++];
        }
    }


    public float peek() {
        if (isEmpty()) {
            System.out.println("You have successfully sold all stocks\n");
            return 0;
        }
        return queueArray[front];
    }


    // if there are any remaining share after the sell, of the specified shares slot, then replace them to the front element.
    public void replace(float n) {  // parsing remaining shares to this parameter called n
        --front;
        queueArray[front] = n;
        ++noOfItems;
        count++;
    }
}

class Hello{
    public static void main(String[] args) throws InterruptedException {
        Queue stockArray = new Queue();
        Queue unitPriceArray = new Queue();
        Scanner scanner1 = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.println("                                                 Welcome to buying and selling program");
//        Thread.sleep(1000);
        System.out.println();
        int days;

        while (true) {
            System.out.print("How many transactions you made: ");
            String days1 = scanner1.nextLine();

            if (days1.isEmpty()) { // if user by mistake press enter button he/she will redirect to top
                System.out.println();
                System.out.println("You can't leave this space blank");
                System.out.println();
                continue;
            }

            try {
                days = Integer.parseInt(days1);
                if (days1.matches("[a-zA-Z]+")) {  // if user enter letters, he/she will redirect to top
                    System.out.println();
                    System.out.println("You can enter only positive whole numbers");
                    System.out.println();
                    continue;
                }
                break;

            } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
                System.out.println(); // if user by mistakenly enter zero or negative number here, he/she will redirect to top
                System.out.println("You can enter only positive whole numbers");
            }

            System.out.println();
        }

        System.out.println();
        stockArray.Queue(days);
        unitPriceArray.Queue(days);
        float capitalGain = 0;

        for (int i = 0; i < days; i++) {
//            Thread.sleep(500);
            System.out.print("                ");
            System.out.print("For bought shares, enter 'buy' " + " ");
//            Thread.sleep(500);
            System.out.print("   For sold shares, enter 'sell' " + " ");
//            Thread.sleep(500);
            System.out.println("   For terminate, enter 'exit' ");
            System.out.println();
//            Thread.sleep(500);
            System.out.print("                                                        Enter your choice: ");
            String choice = scanner1.nextLine();
            if (choice.trim().equalsIgnoreCase("buy")) {
//                Thread.sleep(500);
                System.out.print("Enter number of shares you bought : ");
                float noOfBougthShares = Float.parseFloat(scanner1.nextLine());
//                Thread.sleep(500);
                System.out.print("Enter bought price : ");
                float priceOfboughtShares = Float.parseFloat(scanner1.nextLine());
                stockArray.enqueue(noOfBougthShares);
                unitPriceArray.enqueue(priceOfboughtShares);
                System.out.println();
            } else if (choice.trim().equalsIgnoreCase("sell")) {
//                Thread.sleep(500);
                if (stockArray.queueArray[0] != 0) {
                    System.out.print("Enter number of shares you sold : ");
                    float noOfSellingShares = Float.parseFloat(scanner1.nextLine());
//                    Thread.sleep(500);
                    System.out.print("Enter sold price per share: ");
                    float priceOfSellingShares = Float.parseFloat(scanner1.nextLine());
                    float originalyBoughtShares, originalBoughtPrice;
                    System.out.println();
                    while (noOfSellingShares > 0 && stockArray.peek() != 0) {
                        if (noOfSellingShares >= stockArray.peek()) {
                            originalyBoughtShares = stockArray.dequeue();
                            originalBoughtPrice = unitPriceArray.dequeue();
                            capitalGain += (priceOfSellingShares - originalBoughtPrice) * originalyBoughtShares;
                            noOfSellingShares -= originalyBoughtShares;
                        } else {
                            originalyBoughtShares = stockArray.dequeue();
                            originalBoughtPrice = unitPriceArray.peek();
                            capitalGain += (priceOfSellingShares - originalBoughtPrice) * noOfSellingShares;
                            stockArray.replace(originalyBoughtShares - noOfSellingShares);
                            noOfSellingShares = 0;
                        }
                    }

                    //Thread.sleep(500);
                    System.out.println();
                    System.out.println("Your Capital Gain is: " + capitalGain);
                } else {
//                    Thread.sleep(500);
                    System.out.println();
                    System.out.println("                                                  You have to enter bought shares first");
                    System.out.println();
                    System.out.println("                                                             Program ended !!!");
                }

            } else if (choice.trim().equalsIgnoreCase("exit")) {
                break;

            }  else{
                // if user mistakenly enter wrong inputs to " Enter your choice: ", user will redirect to top of the program
//                Thread.sleep(500);
                System.out.println();
                System.out.println("                                                        Enter a valid choice!!!");
                System.out.println();
                i -= 1; // in for loop "i" is increasing even this else part execute, so we need to subtract one from the current value of "i", if not user is not able to enter his/her all transactions to the program

            }
        }

    }
}

[2023-03-27, 21:42:12] Haleef IIT: public void createCardDeck() {      //initialize a card deck with 52 cards
        this.cardDeck = new ArrayList<>(52);
        String[] suits = {"diamonds", "hearts", "spades", "clubs"};
        for (String suit : suits) {
            String[] ranks = {"2", "3", "4", "5", "6", "7", "8", "9", "10", "jack", "queen", "king", "ace"};
            for (String rank : ranks) {
                Card card = new Card(suit, rank);
                this.cardDeck.add(card);
            }
        }
    }

                case "king" -> suitCards.getCard(i).rank = "13";
                case "ace" -> suitCards.getCard(i).rank = "14";
            }
        }
        int n = suitCards.noOfCards;
        for (int i = 1; i < n; i++) {
            int key = Integer.parseInt(suitCards.getCard(i).rank);
            int j = i-1;
            while (j >= 0 && Integer.parseInt(suitCards.getCard(j).rank) > key){
                Card temp = suitCards.getCard(j+1);
                suitCards.setCard(j+1,suitCards.getCard(j));
                suitCards.setCard(j,temp);
                j = j -1;
            }
            suitCards.getCard(j+1).rank = String.valueOf(key);
        }
        for(int i = 0; i < suitCards.noOfCards; i++){
            switch (suitCards.getCard(i).rank) {
                case "11" -> suitCards.getCard(i).rank = "jack";
                case "12" -> suitCards.getCard(i).rank = "queen";
                case "13" -> suitCards.getCard(i).rank = "king";
                case "14" -> suitCards.getCard(i).rank = "ace";
            }
        }
        return suitCards;

[2023-04-07, 00:13:52] Deelaka Dias: public static void sortPlayerHands() {
        for (Player player : playersArrayList) {
            ArrayList<String> hand = player.getHand();
            int n = hand.size();
            for (int i = 0; i < n - 1; i++) {
                for (int j = 0; j < n - i - 1; j++) {
                    String card1 = hand.get(j);
                    String card2 = hand.get(j + 1);
                    if (card1.compareTo(card2) > 0) {
                        // swap cards
                        hand.set(j, card2);
                        hand.set(j + 1, card1);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
